      <p><img src="/images/main/home.jpg" alt="Heritage" width="640" height="240" /></p> 
      <h3>California Center for Native Nations</h3> 
      <p class="kicker">Inspired by the generosity and vision of Rupert and Jeannette Costo, the California Center for Native Nations (CCNN) at the University of California, Riverside (UCR) was established in 2000. As part of the most diverse UC campus, the CCNN is dedicated to preserving the history, culture, language, and sovereignty of California’s first nations and represents UCR’s ongoing commitment to research and service benefiting California Indians.</p> 
      <p>Housed within the College of Humanities, Arts and Social Sciences, this innovative world-class research center draws upon the academic strengths of distinguished American Indian Studies faculty in the departments of History, Ethnic Studies, English, Religious Studies, Dance, Music, and Anthropology to address issues involving policy, health care, education, arts and culture, economic development and the environment.</p> 
      <div class="l_msg_box" id="l_video"> 
       <iframe title="YouTube Video Player" width="640" height="360" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/qSr6nw9XcMg?rel=0&amp;showinfo=0" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen=""></iframe> 
       <h3>Marigold Linton</h3> 
       <h4>’58 B.A. Psychology, 2012 Distinguished Alumnus Award</h4> 
       <p>A Cahuilla and Cupe&ntilde;o Indian and member of the Morongo Band of Mission Indians, Dr. Linton is the first California reservation Indian to have ever left a (California) reservation to go to a university and is reportedly the 17th American Indian to have ever earned a Ph.D. in any discipline. Her accomplishments include being a founder of the Society for Advancement of Chicanos and Native Americans in Science and the National Indian Education Association, and recipient of the 2009 Presidential Award for Excellence in Science, Mathematics &amp; Engineering Mentoring.</p> 
      </div> 
      <p>Located in the heart of Indian Country, UCR has a lengthy association with Native American studies, students, communities, and tribes. Designed for and with regional tribal leaders, this collaborative partnership provides a platform for issues of critical importance to Native people by offering a comprehensive range of dynamic programs, educational conferences, scholarly research, publications and Web-based media resources. The university offers research fields in Native American Studies where students may earn the B.A. through Ph. D. in American Indian Studies focused in History, Literature, Dance, Music, Ethnic Studies, and Anthropology. In addition, the Costo Library of the American Indian at UCR houses exceptional collections unique in their content dedicated to understanding the history and role of self-determination policy in Indian Country.</p> 
     </div>

      <p class="footer_info"> <img src="/images/ucr_footer.jpg" alt="" width="120" height="103" /> <strong>The University of California, Riverside</strong> (<a href="http://www.ucr.edu/">www.ucr.edu</a>) is a doctoral research university, a living laboratory for groundbreaking exploration of issues critical to Inland Southern California, the state and communities around the world. Reflecting California's diverse culture, UCR’s enrollment has exceeded 21,000 students. The campus will open a medical school in 2013 and has reached the heart of the Coachella Valley by way of the UCR Palm Desert Center. The campus has an annual statewide economic impact of more than $1 billion. </p>

          var swf = "      \u003cembed type=\"application\/x-shockwave-flash\"     s\u0072c=\"http:\/\/s.ytimg.com\/yts\/swfbin\/player-vflISCIWj\/watch_as3.swf\"     name=\"movie_player\"     id=\"movie_player\"    flashvars=\"__flashvars__\"     allowfullscreen=\"true\" allowscriptaccess=\"always\" bgcolor=\"#000000\"\u003e\n  \u003cnoembed\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"yt-alert yt-alert-default yt-alert-error  yt-alert-player\"\u003e  \u003cdiv class=\"yt-alert-icon\"\u003e\n    \u003cimg s\u0072c=\"http:\/\/s.ytimg.com\/yts\/img\/pixel-vfl3z5WfW.gif\" class=\"icon master-sprite\" alt=\"Alert icon\"\u003e\n  \u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"yt-alert-buttons\"\u003e\u003c\/div\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"yt-alert-content\" role=\"alert\"\u003e    \u003cspan class=\"yt-alert-vertical-trick\"\u003e\u003c\/span\u003e\n    \u003cdiv class=\"yt-alert-message\"\u003e\n            You need Adobe Flash Player to watch this video. \u003cbr\u003e \u003ca href=\"http:\/\/get.adobe.com\/flashplayer\/\"\u003eDownload it from Adobe.\u003c\/a\u003e\n    \u003c\/div\u003e\n\u003c\/div\u003e\u003c\/div\u003e\u003c\/noembed\u003e\n\n";
          swf = swf.replace('__flashvars__', encoded.join('&'));
          document.getElementById("player-api").innerHTML = swf;
          ytplayer.config.loaded = true
        })();
      </script>

             <div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-expander yt-uix-expander-collapsed yt-uix-button-panel"> 
              <div id="watch-description-content"> 
               <div id="watch-description-clip"> 
                <p id="watch-uploader-info"> <strong>Published on <span id="eow-date" class="watch-video-date">Sep 24, 2013</span> </strong> </p> 
                <div id="watch-description-text"> 
                 <p id="eow-description">Chancellor Kim A. Wilcox welcomes UC Riverside's newest students to campus, telling them that, &quot;I wish very much that I could talk to each one of you every day to see how it's going. I can't. Instead I have to trust you to go and explore as broadly as you can.&quot; He added that, as opposed to high school, &quot;At a university, we learn together. We all have to lead.&quot;<br /><br />Chancellor Wilcox is introduced by UCR Vice Chancellor, Student Affairs James Sandoval. The ceremony took place at the Student Recreation Center.</p> 
                </div>

        // Google WaterMark Script
        $(function () {
            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {
                ToggleHint($(this)); // add class on page load to elements with "hintable" class
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }
    </script>

     <div class="span-11"> 
      <h3>How to Sign Up For CRAMS Training</h3> 
      <p>Our two-part training sessions are the best way to learn how to submit a course proposal properly. Please <a href="mailto:melinda.miller@ucr.edu" target="_blank">email Course Specialist Melinda Miller</a> to sign up for training. </p> 
      <h3><br /> How to Log in to CRAMS </h3> 
      <p>Training is required for permission to log in to CRAMS (see above). </p> 
      <p> <strong>Preparers</strong></p> 
      <ol> 
       <li>Meet all <a href="/crams/support-services/system-requirements.aspx">system requirements</a>. </li> 
       <li>Double-click the CRAMS icon on your desktop.</li> 
       <li>Enter your UCR Net ID and password and click <strong>OK</strong>.</li> 
      </ol> 
      <p><strong>Approvers</strong></p> 
      <ol> 
       <li>Meet all system requirements.<strong> </strong></li> 
       <li><a href="http://cramsportal.ucr.edu/crams/approver.login" target="_blank">Log in here</a> using your UCR Net ID and password.<strong> </strong></li> 
      </ol> 
      <p><strong>General Users </strong></p> 
      <p>Use the <a href="http://cramsportal.ucr.edu/crams/courses.search" target="_blank">Web-based CRAMS application</a> to view all courses and search for proposals. Logging in is not necessary. Fields cannot be edited in this mode. </p> 
      <h3><br /> How to Update Your Profile </h3> 
      <p> It’s important to keep your contact information (phone number, email) up-to-date in CRAMS because others may need to contact you during the course proposal process. Also, it helps to ensure all auto-fill functions work correctly. <strong>Updating your profile is easy: </strong></p> 
     </div> 
     <div class="span-7 last"> 
      <div class="sidebar"> 
       <img src="/Images/magnifier.png" style="float: right; margin: 4px;" /> 
       <div class="title">
         CRAMS Resources: 
       </div> 
       <ul> 
        <li><a href="/Content/pdfs/Find_a_Preparer.pdf" target="_new">Find a Preparer</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://senate.ucr.edu/committee/8/Submission%20Deadlines%20for%202014-15.pdf">Dates and Deadlines</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/crams/courseproposal/reports.aspx">Request Reports</a></li> 
        <li><a href="http://senate.ucr.edu/committee/?do=info&amp;id=8]">Committee on Courses</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/crams/locationofcourses/default.aspx">Track My Proposal</a></li> 
        <li><a href="/crams/supportservices/cramsfaq.aspx">FAQs (Priority Enrollment, Sunset Clause, NOFY, Cross-Listed)</a></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div>

    <h2>Instructional Technology Group</h2> 
    <!-- Start Sidebar --> 
    <div id="sidebar"> 
     <div class="nav"> 
      <h3 class="accessibility">Main Navigation</h3> 
      <ul> 
       <li><a href="/" title="Home">Home<br /><span></span></a></li>

         <li class="currentpage"><h3><dfn>Current page is: </dfn>Instructional Technology Group</h3></li>
         <li><a href="/mt.html" title="Multimedia Technologies">Multimedia Technologies</a></li>

    <!-- Start Content Area --> 
    <div id="main"> 
     <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/macy.css" cssmenu="" width="790" --> 
     <div class="header"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="title" group="Everyone" button="734" -->
      <!-- com.omniupdate.editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484" --> 
      <!-- /com.omniupdate.div -->
     </div> 
     <div id="omnicontent"> 
      <!-- com.omniupdate.div label="maincontent" group="Everyone" button="657" -->
      <!-- ouc:editor csspath="/z-omniupdate/css/style.css" cssmenu="/z-omniupdate/css/style.txt" width="484"/ -->
      <p>Instructional Technology Group offers faculty and students technological support relating to academic disciplines. We emphasize a &quot;hands-on&quot; approach to our services, whether it's support for courses in Blackboard or support to augment classroom presentations. UCR has also invested in Lynda.com in support of software training.</p> 
      <p>The Instructional Technology component of Instructional Technology Group supports campus faculty by introducing new technologies and by providing access, training, and support in the use of computers and networking in the classroom. By enhancing the instructor's capability to use technology in the classroom as well as out of the lecture hall, we enhance the quality of instruction and support life-long learning and critical thinking among our faculty and students.</p> 
      <h3>Mission Statement</h3> 
      <p>Instructional Technology Group recognizes that instruction is a dynamic, ongoing interchange between instructor and student that can occur both in and outside of the classroom. By introducing, providing access to, and supporting the use of computers by faculty and students, we seek to enhance the quality and quantity of research, instruction and service provided by University faculty.</p> 
      <h3>Services</h3> 
      <ul class="big_links"> 
       <li><a href="/ilearn"><img src="/images/blackboard.gif" alt="iLearn" width="131" height="68" /><strong>iLearn</strong>iLearn is a comprehensive course management system for web-based, on-line academic classes. UCR faculty is fully supported in the use of iLearn with online workshops, on-line reference and self-help guides, and training by appointment.</a></li> 
       <li><a href="http://sitelicense.ucr.edu"><img src="/images/software_site_licensing.jpg" alt="site license" width="131" height="68" /><strong>Software Site Licensing</strong>Computing &amp; Communications site licensing services provides the ability for UCR faculty, staff and students to purchase software at a substantial discount. In many cases we work with other UC campuses and the Office of the President to obtain the best possible pricing.</a></li> 
      </ul> 
      <h3>Staff</h3> 
      <div class="spotlight"> 
       <h3>Instructional Technology Group</h3> 
       <p><a href="http://www.campusmap.ucr.edu/campusMap.php?loc=CCCTR" target="_blank">Computing &amp; Communications Building</a><br /> Office Hours: M-F 8:00a-12:00p 1:00p-6:00p<br /> Phone: (951) 827-3555<br /> Fax: (951) 827-4541<br /> Email:<a href="mailto:helpdesk@ucr.edu"> Help Desk</a></p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="contact-us"> 
       <p><strong>Dr. Leo P. Schouest</strong><br /> Email: <a href="mailto:leo.schouest@ucr.edu">leo.schouest@ucr.edu</a><br /> (951) 827-3555</p> 
       <p>Dr. Schouest has been with the UCR campus for over 20 years and has in the last three years successfully implemented many IT principles within the Science environment. With a total of 30 years experience in higher education at both private and public research and teaching institutions, he provides a balanced and academic-centered perspective to the Instructional Technology Group mission.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="contact-us"> 
       <p><strong>Dr. Ming Yang</strong><br /> Email: <a href="mailto:ming.yang@ucr.edu">ming.yang@ucr.edu</a><br /> (951) 827-3555</p> 
       <p>With a Ph.D. in Educational Administration with a research emphasis in Instructional Design, Dr Yang has extensive experience in multimedia integration of instructional content in the classroom. He has implemented Distance Learning and multi-campus delivery models for several years.</p> 
      </div> 
      <div class="contact-us"> 
       <p><strong>Dr. Mark A. Nicolay</strong><br /> Email: <a href="mailto:mark.nicolay@ucr.edu">mark.nicolay@ucr.edu</a><br /> (951) 827-3555</p> 
       <p>Dr. Nicolay earned the Doctor of Musical Arts degree from USC in 1989. With experience in Music and Fine Arts computer applications, he brings a creative component to Instructional Technology Group. He is also the campus site license coordinator and has extensive experience in most software licensing aspects.</p> 
      </div>
